    var data = {data}
    var chart = klinecharts.init("chart")
    chart.setStyles("dark")
    chart.setStyles({
      grid: {
        show: true,
        horizontal: {
          show: true,
          size: 1,
          color: "#1a1b1f",
          style: "fill",
        },
        vertical: {
          show: true,
          size: 1,
          color: "#1a1b1f",
          style: "fill",
        }
      },
      candle: {
        bar: {
          upColor: "#dc4546",
          upBorderColor: "#dc4546",
          upWickColor: "#dc4546",
          downColor: "#19a96f",
          downBorderColor: "#19a96f",
          downWickColor: "#19a96f",
        },
        tooltip: {
          custom: [
            { title: "time", value: "{time}" },
            { title: "open", value: "{open}" },
            { title: "high", value: "{high}" },
            { title: "low", value: "{low}" },
            { title: "close", value: "{close}" }
          ]
        },
        priceMark: {
          show: true,

    var data = data.reverse().map(function (data) {
      return {
        timestamp: new Date(data.time).getTime(),
        open: data.open,
        high: data.high,
        low: data.low,
        close: data.close,
      }
    })
    chart.applyNewData(data)
    klinecharts.registerOverlay({
      name: "mark",
      lock: true,
      createPointFigures: function (a) {
        let { coordinates, overlay } = a;
        let x = coordinates[2].x
        let y = coordinates[2].y
        let high = coordinates[0].y
        let low = coordinates[1].y
        let text = overlay.extendData.text
        let flag = text.indexOf("BuyLong") != -1 || text.indexOf("BuySell") != -1
        return [
          {
            type: "polygon",
            attrs: {
              coordinates: [
                {
                  x: x,
                  y: y
                },
                {
                  x: flag ?  x - 10 : x + 10,
                  y: y - 10
                },
                {
                  x: flag ? x - 10 : x + 10,
                  y: y + 10
                },
                {
                  x: x,
                  y: y
                },
              ]
            },
            styles: {
              style: "fill",
              color: flag ? "red" : "lime",
            }
          },
          {
            type: "polygon",
            attrs: {
              coordinates: [
                {
                  x: x,
                  y: flag ? low + 10 : high - 10
                },
                {
                  x: x - 10,
                  y: flag ? low + 20 : high - 20
                },
                {
                  x: x - 4,
                  y: flag ? low + 20 : high - 20
                },
                {
                  x: x - 4,
                  y: flag ? low + 40 : high - 40
                },
                {
                  x: x + 4,
                  y: flag ? low + 40 : high - 40
                },
                {
                  x: x + 4,
                  y: flag ? low + 20 : high - 20
                },
                {
                  x: x + 10,
                  y: flag ? low + 20 : high - 20
                },
              ]
            },
            styles: {
              style: "fill",
              color: flag ? "red" : "lime",
            }
          },
          {
            type: "text",
            attrs: {
              x: x,
              y: flag ? low + 60 : high - 60,
              text: text,
              align: "center",
              baseline: "middle"
            }
          }
        ]
      }
    })
    function mark(time, text, value) {
      let data = this.data.findLast(v => v.timestamp <= time);
      chart.createOverlay({
      name: "mark",
      extendData: {
        text: text,
        high: data.high,
        low: data.low
      },
      points: [
          { timestamp: data.timestamp, value: data.high },
          { timestamp: data.timestamp, value: data.low },
          { timestamp: data.timestamp, value: value }
        ],
      })
    }
    {mark}
  </script>
